"diagnoses of abnormalities of heart beat\u00a0\u00a0. in this classification, this covers the group of activities that yields a diagnosis of abnormalities of heart beat. abnormalities of heart beat is listed in the world health organizations international statistical classification of diseases and related health problems (icd-10) as a four-character category under code r00. icd-10 also has the following abnormalities of heart beat children in its four-character category: r00.0 (tachycardia, unspecified); r00.1 (bradycardia, unspecified); r00.2 (palpitations); r00.8 (other and unspecified abnormalities of heart beat). . "

"diagnoses of symptoms and signs involving appearance and behaviour\u00a0\u00a0. in this classification, this covers the group of activities that yields a diagnosis of symptoms and signs involving appearance and behaviour. symptoms and signs involving appearance and behaviour is listed in the world health organizations international statistical classification of diseases and related health problems (icd-10) as a four-character category under code r46. icd-10 also has the following symptoms and signs involving appearance and behaviour children in its four-character category: r46.0 (very low level of personal hygiene); r46.1 (bizarre personal appearance); r46.2 (strange and inexplicable behaviour); r46.3 (overactivity); r46.4 (slowness and poor responsiveness); r46.5 (suspiciousness and marked evasiveness); r46.6 (undue concern and preoccupation with stressful events); r46.7 (verbosity and circumstantial detail obscuring reason for contact); r46.8 (other symptoms and signs involving appearance and behaviour); r47.0 (dysphasia and aphasia); r47.1 (dysarthria and anarthria); r47.8 (other and unspecified speech disturbances). . r82.7 (abnormal findings on microbiological examination of urine); r82.8 (abnormal findings on cytological and histological examination of urine); r82.9 (other and unspecified abnormal findings in urine); r83.0 (abnormal findings in cerebrospinal fluid : abnormal level of enzymes); r83.1 (abnormal findings in cerebrospinal fluid : abnormal level of hormones); r83.2 (abnormal findings in cerebrospinal fluid : abnormal level of other drugs, medicaments and biological substances); r83.3 (abnormal findings in cerebrospinal fluid : abnormal level of substances chiefly nonmedicinal as to source); r83.4 (abnormal findings in cerebrospinal fluid : abnormal immunological findings); r83.5 (abnormal findings in cerebrospinal fluid : abnormal microbiological findings); r83.6 (abnormal findings in cerebrospinal fluid : abnormal cytological findings); r83.7 (abnormal findings in cerebrospinal fluid : abnormal histological findings); r83.8 (abnormal findings in cerebrospinal fluid : other abnormal findings); r83.9 (abnormal findings in cerebrospinal fluid : unspecified abnormal finding). the diagnosis of myoglobinuria\u00a0\u00a0. in this classification, this covers the group of activities that yields a diagnosis of myoglobinuria. myoglobinuria is listed in the world health organizations international statistical classification of diseases and related health problems (icd-10) as a four-character category under code r82.1..
